<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подонок.html>подо́нок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podónok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подонок.html>подо́нка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подонок.html>подо́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подонок.html>подо́нков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rogue, bastard, rat, scum, scoundrel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подонок.html>подо́нки</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:общество.html>о́бщества</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podónki</b> óbščestva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">scum of society, dregs of society</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опека.html>опе́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">opéka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опыт.html>о́пыт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ópyt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подорвать.html>подорва́ть</a> (10883)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подорвать.html>подорва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podorvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подрывать.html>подрыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blow up, to blast</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to undermine, to sap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подорвать.html>подорва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:здоровье.html>здоро́вье</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podorvátʹ</b> zdoróvʹje (síly)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to undermine one's health (strength)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подорвать.html>подорва́ть</a></b> че́й-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:авторитет.html>авторите́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podorvátʹ</b> čéj-libo avtoritét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to undermine smb's authority</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подорвать.html>подорва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:доверие.html>дове́рие</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podorvátʹ</b> dovérije kovó-libo k komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shake someone's faith in someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подорвать.html>подорва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:экономика.html>эконо́мику</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podorvátʹ</b> ekonómiku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to undermine the economy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подорвать.html>подорва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мощь.html>мощь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podorvátʹ</b> vojénnuju moščʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to undermine/sap the military power</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подрыв.html>подры́в</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podrýv</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подрывник.html>подрывни́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podryvník</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подорваться.html>подорва́ться</a> (24042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подорвать.html>подорва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podorvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подорваться.html>подорва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podorvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подрыва́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to explode, to blow up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be damaged, to deteriorate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> neologism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suddenly start (doing something)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> neologism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be determined (to do something)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подорвать.html>подорва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podorvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***подорожать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подорожать.html>подорожа́ть</a> (23579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорожать.html>дорожа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dorožátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подорожать.html>подорожа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podorožátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорожать.html>дорожа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rise in price, to go up</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вздорожа́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vzdorožátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***подослать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подослать.html>подосла́ть</a> (3259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слать.html>слать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подослать.html>подосла́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podoslátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подсыла́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to send something <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">secretly</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подоспеть.html>подоспе́ть</a> (9201)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спеть.html>спеть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spetʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подоспеть.html>подоспе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podospétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подоспева́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come/arrive/be in time <i>(for)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(time)</i> to come, to arrive</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be mature/ripe</li></ol>

***подохнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подохнуть.html>подо́хнуть</a> (12428)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дохнуть.html>до́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dóxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подохнуть.html>подо́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podóxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дохнуть.html>до́хнуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подыхать.html>подыха́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(animals)</i> to die, to fall</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to peg out, to kick the bucket, to croak</li></ol>

***подошва.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подошва.html>подо́шва</a> (5621)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">подъшьва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podŭšĭva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sole (bottom); foundation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*šiti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The doublet <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">póčva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> might have arisen from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> genitive plural <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">подъшьвъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podŭšĭvŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, giving <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> genitive plural <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">почевъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">počev</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">póčva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> by analogical levelling.</li></ul>
<ul><li>Another possibility is that both <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подошва.html>подо́шва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podóšva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">póčva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> come from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*podъšьvь</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">počev</i>), which would yield nominative <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*подшевь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*podševʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> ~ genitive <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*подошви</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*podošvi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, each giving rise, after transfer into a-stem, to a complete levelled paradigm.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подошва.html>подо́шва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podóšva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подошва.html>подо́швы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подошва.html>подо́швы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подошва.html>подо́шв</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sole <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">bottom of the foot or of the shoe</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>foot <i>(of the mountain)</i></li></ol>

***подпадать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпадать.html>подпада́ть</a> (31577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подпа́д-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podpád-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подпадать.html>подпада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podpadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подпа́сть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall <i>(under)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подпадать.html>подпада́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> чьё-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:влияние.html>влия́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podpadátʹ</b> po čʹjó-libo vlijánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall under smb's influence</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***подпевавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпевать.html>подпева́вший</a> (18442)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подпевать.html>подпева́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podpevávšij</span>)
</p>

***подпевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпевать.html>подпева́ть</a> (18442)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подпе́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podpétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>петь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">petʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подпевать.html>подпева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podpevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подпе́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sing the supporting part <i>(in a duet or choir)</i>, to sing backup</li>
<li>to sing along <i>(with)</i>, to harmonize <i>(with)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> deprecative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to echo</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпирать.html>подпираемый</a> (11574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подписавший.html>подписа́вший</a> (1953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подписавший.html>подписа́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podpisávšij</span>)
</p>

***подписать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подписать.html>подписа́ть</a> (1953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подписать.html>подписа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podpisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подписывать.html>подпи́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sign <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">one's own name</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забы́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подписать.html>подписа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочинение.html>сочине́ние</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja zabýl <b>podpisátʹ</b> svojó sočinénije.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I forgot <b>to sign</b> my essay.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to add to</li>
<li>to subscribe, to take out a subscription for someone</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The verb, <a href = vnd.unilang:подписать.html>подписа́ть</a>, may be directly translated as "to subscribe" word by word. For instance,
</p>
<ul><li><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> = sub- (often as "under, beneath")</li>
<li><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> = scribe</li></ul>
<p>However, this does not mean "a sense of writing something under a body of texts".
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нижеподписавшийся</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nižepodpisavšijsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подписка.html>подпи́ска</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podpíska</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подписчик.html>подпи́счик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podpísčik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подпись.html>по́дпись</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pódpisʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:подписать.html>Подписа́ть</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несколько.html>не́сколько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:строка.html>стро́к</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сделать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подписчик.html>подпи́счиком</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:абонент.html>абоне́нтом</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подписка.html>подпи́ска</a> (9360)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подписка.html>подпи́ска</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podpíska</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подписка.html>подпи́ски</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подписка.html>подпи́ски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подписка.html>подпи́сок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>subscription
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приниматься.html>принима́ется</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подписка.html>подпи́ска</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:газета.html>газе́ты</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prinimájetsja <b>podpíska</b> na gazéty</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">subscriptions to newspapers are accepted</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подписка.html>подпи́ску</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on dal v étom <b>podpísku</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he made a signed statement to the effect</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
